focus = {
	id = SOV_Introduce_NEP
	text = RUS_Introduce_NEP
	icon = GFX_RUS_Introduce_NEP
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = { focus = SOV_Milestone_Highway_To_Socialism }
	relative_position_id = SOV_Premier_Bukharin
	x = 0
	y = 2
	available = {
		SOV_bukharin_in_power = yes
	}
	bypass = { 
		hidden_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_bypass_nep
				has_country_flag = SOV_decided_to_go_down_with_nep
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_New_Economic_Policy_modifier }
			}
		}
	}
	bypass_effect = {	
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_New_Economic_Policy_modifier } }
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_New_Economic_Policy_modifier }		
		}
		complete_national_focus = RUS_Revive_Market_Elements
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = russoc.160
				days = 20
			}
			country_event = {
				id = russoc.123
				days = 70
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rusdem.314
				days = 35
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOV_Introduce_NEP"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = rus_unfinished_land_reform
			}
			destroy_unfinished_land_reform = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		country_event = rusdem.309
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_New_Economic_Policy_modifier }
		complete_national_focus = RUS_Revive_Market_Elements
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = russoc.160
				days = 20
			}
			country_event = {
				id = russoc.123
				days = 70
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rusdem.314
				days = 35
			}
		}	
	}
}

focus = {
	id = SOV_Smychka
	text = RUS_Smychka
	icon = GFX_RUS_Promote_Smychka
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = { focus = SOV_Introduce_NEP }
	relative_position_id = SOV_Premier_Bukharin
	x = -1
	y = 3
	available = {
		SOV_bukharin_in_power = yes
	}
	bypass = { 
		hidden_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_bypass_nep
				has_country_flag = SOV_decided_to_go_down_with_nep
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 40 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOV_Smychka"
		country_event = rusdem.312
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = RUS_upk }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { RUS_nep_worker > RUS_nep_peasant } }
			RUS_nep_increase_peasant = yes
		}
		else = {
			RUS_nep_increase_worker = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_modify_nep
		add_to_variable = { 
			RUS_NEP_stability_factor = 0.05 
			tooltip = stability_tooltip
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			RUS_NEP_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = 0.03 
			tooltip = production_factory_max_efficiency_factor_tooltip
		}		
	}
}

	shared_focus = {
		id = RUS_SOV_Modernise_The_Petrograd_Dockyards
		text = RUS_Modernise_The_Petrograd_Dockyards
		icon = GFX_RUS_Modernise_Petrograd_Dockyards
		available = {
			195 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		relative_position_id = RUS_SOV_Take_To_The_Seas
		x = 1
		y = 1
		cost = 8
		prerequisite = {
			focus = RUS_SOV_Take_To_The_Seas
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					has_war_with = USA
					has_war_with = TEX
					has_war_with = CAL
					has_war_with = CAN
					has_war_with = JAP
				}
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus RUS_SOV_Modernise_The_Petrograd_Dockyards"
			195 = { #Petrograd
				if = {
					limit = { can_construct_building = naval_facility }
					add_building_construction = {
						type = naval_facility
						level = 1
						province = 6174 #Petrograd
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { extra_facility = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { free_building_slots = { building = dockyard size > 2 include_locked = yes } }
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 3
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { free_building_slots = { building = dockyard size > 1 include_locked = yes } }
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
					set_temp_variable = { extra_dockyards = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { free_building_slots = { building = dockyard size > 0 include_locked = yes } }
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
					set_temp_variable = { extra_dockyards = 2 }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { extra_dockyards = 3 }
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = naval_base
					level = 3
					province = 6174
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { extra_dockyards > 0 } }
				add_one_random_dockyard = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { extra_dockyards > 1 } }
				add_one_random_dockyard = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { extra_dockyards > 2 } }
				add_one_random_dockyard = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = extra_facility }
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						can_construct_building = naval_facility
					}
					construct_building_in_random_province = { naval_facility = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
